(**
 1. Final object
 *)

is_bifinal unit_category


is_bifinal unit_category

  
bifinal_1cell_property unit_category
∏ Y : bicat_of_univ_cats,
bifinal_2cell_property unit_category Y
∏ Y : bicat_of_univ_cats,
bifinal_eq_property unit_category Y

  
bifinal_1cell_property unit_category
 exact (λ C, functor_to_unit (pr1 C)).
  
∏ Y : bicat_of_univ_cats,
bifinal_2cell_property unit_category Y
 exact (λ C F G, unit_category_nat_trans F G).
  
∏ Y : bicat_of_univ_cats,
bifinal_eq_property unit_category Y
 
Y: bicat_of_univ_cats
f, g: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ Y, unit_category ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
α = β

    apply nat_trans_to_unit_eq.
Defined.

Definition bifinal_cats
  : bifinal_obj bicat_of_univ_cats
  := unit_category ,, is_bifinal_cats.

  Section CellUMP.
    Let p := iso_comma_pb_cone F G.

    Context {q : bicat_of_univ_cats}
            (φ ψ : q --> p)
            (α : φ · pb_cone_pr1 p ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr1 p)
            (β : φ · pb_cone_pr2 p ==> ψ · pb_cone_pr2 p)
            (r : (φ ◃ pb_cone_cell p)
                 • lassociator _ _ _
                 • (β ▹ G)
                 • rassociator _ _ _
                 =

C: bicat_of_univ_cats
φ, ψ: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C, iso_comma_pb_cone F G ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)
r: (((φ ◃ pb_cone_cell (iso_comma_pb_cone F G))
  • lassociator φ
      (pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) G)
 • (β ▹ G))
• rassociator ψ
    (pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) G =
((lassociator φ
    (pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) F
  • (α ▹ F))
 • rassociator ψ
     (pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) F)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell (iso_comma_pb_cone F G))
pb_ump_2_nat_trans φ ψ α β r
▹ pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) = α
 exact (pb_ump_2_nat_trans_pr1 φ ψ α β r).
        
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₃ ⟧
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
C: bicat_of_univ_cats
φ, ψ: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C, iso_comma_pb_cone F G ⟧
α: φ · pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)
β: φ · pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) ==>
ψ · pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)
r: (((φ ◃ pb_cone_cell (iso_comma_pb_cone F G))
  • lassociator φ
      (pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) G)
 • (β ▹ G))
• rassociator ψ
    (pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) G =
((lassociator φ
    (pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) F
  • (α ▹ F))
 • rassociator ψ
     (pb_cone_pr1 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)) F)
• (ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell (iso_comma_pb_cone F G))
pb_ump_2_nat_trans φ ψ α β r
▹ pb_cone_pr2 (iso_comma_pb_cone F G) = β
 exact (pb_ump_2_nat_trans_pr2 φ ψ α β r).
  Defined.

has_pb_ump (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)

 exact pb_ump_1_iso_comma.

  Defined.
End IsoCommaUMP.


has_pb bicat_of_univ_cats


has_pb bicat_of_univ_cats

G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
∑ p : pb_cone F G, has_pb_ump p

pb_cone F G

G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
(λ p : pb_cone F G, has_pb_ump p) ?pr1

pb_cone F G
 exact (iso_comma_pb_cone F G).

(λ p : pb_cone F G, has_pb_ump p)
  (iso_comma_pb_cone F G)
 exact (iso_comma_has_pb_ump F G).
Defined.

(**
 4. Strict pullbacks
 *)
Section ReindexingPullback.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats}
          (F : C₁ --> C₂)
          (D₂ : disp_univalent_category (pr1 C₂))
          (HD₂ : iso_cleaving (pr1 D₂)).

  Let tot_D₂ : bicat_of_univ_cats
    := total_univalent_category D₂.
  Let pb : bicat_of_univ_cats
    := univalent_reindex_cat F D₂.
  Let π₁ : pb --> _
    := pr1_category _.
  Let π₂ : pb --> tot_D₂
    := total_functor (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F D₂).
  Let γ : invertible_2cell (π₁ · F) (π₂ · pr1_category D₂)
    := nat_z_iso_to_invertible_2cell
         (π₁ · F)
         (π₂ · pr1_category D₂)
         (total_functor_commute_z_iso (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F (pr1 D₂))).
  Let cone : pb_cone F (pr1_category _ : tot_D₂ --> C₂)
    := make_pb_cone pb π₁ π₂ γ.

(((lassociator (reindexing_has_pb_ump_1_cell q)

    ▹ pr1_category D₂))

    (pb_cone_pr2 cone) (pr1_category D₂)

C₀: bicat_of_univ_cats
G₁, G₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₀, cone ⟧
τ₁: G₁ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> G₂ · pb_cone_pr1 cone
τ₂: G₁ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> G₂ · pb_cone_pr2 cone
p: (((G₁ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
  • lassociator G₁ (pb_cone_pr2 cone)
      (pr1_category D₂)) • 
 (τ₂ ▹ pr1_category D₂))
• rassociator G₂ (pb_cone_pr2 cone)
    (pr1_category D₂) =
((lassociator G₁ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) F • (τ₁ ▹ F))
 • rassociator G₂ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) F)
• (G₂ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
∃! γ : G₁ ==> G₂,
γ ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = τ₁ × γ ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = τ₂

γ:= nat_z_iso_to_invertible_2cell 
  (π₁ · F) (π₂ · pr1_category D₂)
  (total_functor_commute_z_iso
     (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F (pr1 D₂))): invertible_2cell (π₁ · F) (π₂ · pr1_category D₂)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb π₁ π₂ γ: pb_cone F
  (pr1_category D₂
   :
   bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ tot_D₂, C₂ ⟧)
C₀: bicat_of_univ_cats
G₁, G₂: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₀, cone ⟧
τ₁: G₁ · pb_cone_pr1 cone ==> G₂ · pb_cone_pr1 cone
τ₂: G₁ · pb_cone_pr2 cone ==> G₂ · pb_cone_pr2 cone
p: (((G₁ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
  • lassociator G₁ (pb_cone_pr2 cone)
      (pr1_category D₂)) • 
 (τ₂ ▹ pr1_category D₂))
• rassociator G₂ (pb_cone_pr2 cone)
    (pr1_category D₂) =
((lassociator G₁ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) F • (τ₁ ▹ F))
 • rassociator G₂ (pb_cone_pr1 cone) F)
• (G₂ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
(λ _ : reindex_pb_ump_2 F (pr1 D₂) G₁ G₂ τ₁ τ₂
         (reindexing_has_pb_ump_2_subproof0 C₀ G₁ G₂
            τ₁ τ₂ p) ▹ pb_cone_pr1 cone = τ₁,
 reindex_pb_ump_2 F (pr1 D₂) G₁ G₂ τ₁ τ₂
   (reindexing_has_pb_ump_2_subproof0 C₀ G₁ G₂ τ₁ τ₂ p)
 ▹ pb_cone_pr2 cone = τ₂)
  (reindex_pb_ump_2_pr1 F (pr1 D₂) G₁ G₂ τ₁ τ₂
     (reindexing_has_pb_ump_2_subproof0 C₀ G₁ G₂ τ₁ τ₂
        p))
 apply reindex_pb_ump_2_pr2.
  Defined.

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
D₂: disp_univalent_category (pr1 C₂)
HD₂: iso_cleaving (pr1 D₂)
tot_D₂:= total_univalent_category D₂: bicat_of_univ_cats

     (comma_cone_pr1 comma_comma_cone) F

           (comma_cone_pr2 q) (comma_cone_cell q)
         · comma_cone_pr1 comma_comma_cone)

        (comma_ump1_pr1 F G (comma_cone_pr1 q)
           (comma_cone_pr2 q) (comma_cone_cell q)) ▹ F))
  • comma_cone_cell q)

       (comma_ump1 F G (comma_cone_pr1 q)
          (comma_cone_pr2 q) (comma_cone_cell q)
        · comma_cone_pr2 comma_comma_cone)

       (comma_ump1_pr2 F G (comma_cone_pr1 q)
          (comma_cone_pr2 q) (comma_cone_cell q))) ^-1
    ▹ G))
• rassociator
    (comma_ump1 F G (comma_cone_pr1 q)
       (comma_cone_pr2 q) (comma_cone_cell q))
    (comma_cone_pr2 comma_comma_cone) G
 abstract
        (use nat_trans_eq ; [ apply homset_property | ] ;
         intro x ; cbn ; unfold pb_cone_cell ;
         rewrite (functor_id F), (functor_id G) ;
         rewrite !id_left, !id_right ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

  Section CellUMP.
    Let p := comma_comma_cone.

    Context {q : bicat_of_univ_cats}
            (φ ψ : q --> p)
            (α : φ · comma_cone_pr1 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr1 p)
            (β : φ · comma_cone_pr2 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr2 p)
            (r : (φ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)
                 • lassociator _ _ _
                 • (β ▹ G)
                 • rassociator _ _ _
                 =
                 lassociator _ _ _
                 • (α ▹ F)
                 • rassociator _ _ _
                 • (ψ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)).

    
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₃ ⟧
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
p:= comma_comma_cone: comma_cone F G
q: bicat_of_univ_cats
φ, ψ: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ q, p ⟧
α: φ · comma_cone_pr1 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr1 p
β: φ · comma_cone_pr2 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr2 p
r: (((φ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)
  • lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr2 p) G) • (β ▹ G))
• rassociator ψ (comma_cone_pr2 p) G =
((lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr1 p) F • (α ▹ F))
 • rassociator ψ (comma_cone_pr1 p) F)
• (ψ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)
φ ==> ψ

    
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₃ ⟧
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
p:= comma_comma_cone: comma_cone F G
q: bicat_of_univ_cats
φ, ψ: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ q, p ⟧
α: φ · comma_cone_pr1 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr1 p
β: φ · comma_cone_pr2 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr2 p
r: (((φ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)
  • lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr2 p) G) • (β ▹ G))
• rassociator ψ (comma_cone_pr2 p) G =
((lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr1 p) F • (α ▹ F))
 • rassociator ψ (comma_cone_pr1 p) F)
• (ψ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)
φ ==> ψ

      
C₁, C₂, C₃: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₃ ⟧
G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₂, C₃ ⟧
p:= comma_comma_cone: comma_cone F G
q: bicat_of_univ_cats
φ, ψ: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ q, p ⟧
α: φ · comma_cone_pr1 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr1 p
β: φ · comma_cone_pr2 p ==> ψ · comma_cone_pr2 p
r: (((φ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)
  • lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr2 p) G) • (β ▹ G))
• rassociator ψ (comma_cone_pr2 p) G =
((lassociator φ (comma_cone_pr1 p) F • (α ▹ F))
 • rassociator ψ (comma_cone_pr1 p) F)
• (ψ ◃ comma_cone_cell p)
∏ x : q, pr2 (φ x) · # G (β x) = # F (α x) · pr2 (ψ x)

      abstract
        (intros x ;
         pose (nat_trans_eq_pointwise r x) as z ;
         cbn in z ;
         unfold iso_comma_commute_nat_trans_data in z ;
         rewrite !id_left, !id_right in z ;
         exact z).
    Defined.

Definition has_comma_bicat_of_univ_cats
  : has_comma bicat_of_univ_cats
  := λ C₁ C₂ C₃ F G, comma_comma_cone F G ,, comma_has_ump F G.

    (inserter_cone_cell q)
  ◃ inserter_cone_cell (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G))
 • lassociator
     (nat_trans_to_dialgebra (inserter_cone_pr1 q)
        (inserter_cone_cell q))
     (inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G))
     G)
• (nat_z_iso_to_invertible_2cell
     (nat_trans_to_dialgebra (inserter_cone_pr1 q)
        (inserter_cone_cell q)
      · inserter_cone_pr1
          (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G))
     (inserter_cone_pr1 q)
     (nat_trans_to_dialgebra_pr1_nat_z_iso
        (inserter_cone_pr1 q) (inserter_cone_cell q))
   ▹ G) =
(lassociator
   (nat_trans_to_dialgebra (inserter_cone_pr1 q)
      (inserter_cone_cell q))
   (inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)) F
 • (nat_z_iso_to_invertible_2cell
      (nat_trans_to_dialgebra (inserter_cone_pr1 q)
         (inserter_cone_cell q)
       · inserter_cone_pr1
           (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G))
      (inserter_cone_pr1 q)
      (nat_trans_to_dialgebra_pr1_nat_z_iso
         (inserter_cone_pr1 q) (inserter_cone_cell q))
    ▹ F)) • inserter_cone_cell q
 abstract
      (use nat_trans_eq ; [ apply homset_property | ] ;
       intro x ; cbn ;
       rewrite !(functor_id F), !(functor_id G) ;
       rewrite !id_left, !id_right ;
       apply idpath).

n₁, n₂: K₁ ==> K₂
q₁: n₁
▹ inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G) =
α
q₂: n₂
▹ inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G) =
α
x: C₀
n₁ x = n₂ x

F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
C₀: bicat_of_univ_cats

dialgebra_inserter_cone F G ⟧
α: K₁
· inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G) ==>
K₂
· inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)
p: ((rassociator K₁
    (inserter_cone_pr1
       (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)) F
  • (K₁
     ◃ inserter_cone_cell
         (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)))
 • lassociator K₁
     (inserter_cone_pr1
        (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)) G)
• (α ▹ G) =
(((α ▹ F)
  • rassociator K₂
      (inserter_cone_pr1
         (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)) F)
 • (K₂
    ◃ inserter_cone_cell
        (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)))
• lassociator K₂
    (inserter_cone_pr1
       (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G)) G
n₁, n₂: K₁ ==> K₂
q₁: n₁
▹ inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G) =
α
q₂: n₂
▹ inserter_cone_pr1 (dialgebra_inserter_cone F G) =
α
x: C₀
pr1 (n₁ x) = pr1 (n₂ x)

  exact (nat_trans_eq_pointwise q₁ x @ !(nat_trans_eq_pointwise q₂ x)).
Qed.

has_iso_inserters bicat_of_univ_cats


has_iso_inserters bicat_of_univ_cats

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
∑ (i : bicat_of_univ_cats)
(m : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ i, C₁ ⟧)
(α : invertible_2cell (m · F) (m · G)),
has_iso_inserter_ump (make_iso_inserter_cone i m α)

  
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
bicat_of_univ_cats
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ ?pr1, C₁ ⟧
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats

  : bicat_has_em bicat_of_univ_cats
